<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the accordion anatomy and part names.</p>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the accordion package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> accordion</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/accordion&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The accordion package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:accordion/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" <p>You may have noticed we wrapped each accordion trigger within an <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">h3</code>. This is
recommended by the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-practices-1.1/#wai-aria-roles-states-and-properties" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">WAI-ARIA</a>
design pattern to ensure the accordion has the appropriate hierarchy on the
page.</p>
<h3 id="opening-multiple-items" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Opening multiple items<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#opening-multiple-items"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to allow more than one expanded item at a time.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">multiple</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-initial-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> to define expanded items on first render.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// multiple mode</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;home&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;about&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// single mode</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;home&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-accordions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled accordions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-accordions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> to control expanded items externally.</p>

</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">      value <span class="token operator">=</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript"></span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>script</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<h3 id="making-items-collapsible" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Making items collapsible<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#making-items-collapsible"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collapsible</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to allow closing an expanded item by clicking it
again.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Note: If <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code> is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>, we internally set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collapsible</code> to be <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">collapsible</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-value-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for value changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-value-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the accordion value changes, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> callback is invoked.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;selected accordion:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-focus-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for focus changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-focus-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusChange</code> to react when keyboard focus moves between item triggers.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onFocusChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string | null }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;focused item:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="horizontal-orientation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Horizontal orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#horizontal-orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">horizontal</code> when rendering items side by side.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;horizontal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabling-an-accordion-item" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling an accordion item<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-an-accordion-item"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To disable a specific accordion item, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled: true</code> property to the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItemProps</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItemTriggerProps</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItemContentProps</code>.</p>
<p>When an accordion item is disabled, it is skipped from keyboard navigation and
can&#x27;t be interacted with.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getItemProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>h3</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getItemTriggerProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">      Trigger
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>button</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>h3</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getItemContentProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    Content
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text"></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>You can also disable the entire accordion by setting <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code> on the machine.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="open-and-closed-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and closed state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-closed-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an accordion item expands or collapses, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> is set to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code> or
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closed</code> on the item, trigger, and content elements.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item is open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item is open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item-content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item is open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an accordion item&#x27;s trigger is focused, a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code> attribute is set on
the item and content.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the item&#x27;s focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item-trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token pseudo-class">:focus</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the trigger&#x27;s focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item-content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for the content&#x27;s focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="creating-a-component" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Creating a component<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#creating-a-component"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Create your accordion component by abstracting the machine into your own
component.</p>
<h3 id="usage-1" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:accordion/component.usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div <h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The accordion&#x27;s <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods and properties:</p>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The accordion machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; item: (value: string) =&gt; string; itemContent: (value: string) =&gt; string; itemTrigger: (value: string) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the accordion. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether multiple accordion items can be expanded at the same time.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collapsible</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether an accordion item can be closed after it has been expanded.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the expanded accordion items.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the expanded accordion items.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the accordion.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the accordion items are disabled</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">The callback fired when the state of expanded/collapsed accordion items changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: FocusChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">The callback fired when the focused accordion item changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;horizontal&quot; | &quot;vertical&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The orientation of the accordion items.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The accordion <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focusedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The value of the focused accordion item.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The value of the accordion</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the value of the accordion</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getItemState</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(props: ItemProps) =&gt; ItemState</code><span class="d_block">Returns the state of an accordion item.</span></li></ul>

\"@zag-js/accordion\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe accordion package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e so generated element ids stay predictable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"accordion/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou may have noticed we wrapped each accordion trigger within an \u003ccode\u003eh3\u003c/code\u003e. This is\nrecommended by the\n\u003ca href=\"https://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-practices-1.1/#wai-aria-roles-states-and-properties\"\u003eWAI-ARIA\u003c/a\u003e\ndesign pattern to ensure the accordion has the appropriate hierarchy on the\npage.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eOpening multiple items\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003emultiple\u003c/code\u003e to useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  multiple: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e to define expanded items on first render.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e// multiple mode\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  multiple: true,\n  defaultValue: [\"home\", \"about\"],\n})\n\n// single mode\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [\"home\"],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled accordions\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e to control expanded items externally.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"accordion/controlled.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eMaking items collapsible\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003ecollapsible\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e to allow closing an expanded item by clicking \u003ccode\u003ecollapsible\u003c/code\u003e to be \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the accordion value changes, the \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e callback is invoked.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-5}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[] }\n    console.log(\"selected \"horizontal\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisabling an accordion item\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo disable a specific accordion item, pass the \u003ccode\u003edisabled: true\u003c/code\u003e property to the\n\u003ccode\u003egetItemProps\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003egetItemTriggerProps\u003c/code\u003e and with.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e//...\n\u0026#x3C;div {...api.getItemProps({ value: \"item\", disabled: true })}\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;h3\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;button {...api.getItemTriggerProps({ value: \"item\", disabled: true })}\u003e\n      Trigger\n    \u0026#x3C;/button\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;/h3\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getItemContentProps({ value: \"item\", disabled: true })}\u003e\n    Content\n  \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n\u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n//...\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  disabled: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eStyling guide\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a for the item is open or closed state */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eFocused state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen an accordion item's trigger is focused, a headings containing a\ntitle, content snippet, or thumbnail representing a section of content.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/accordion\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Accordion\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Full keyboard navigation\n- Supports single and multiple expanded items\n- Supports collapsible items\n- Supports horizontal and vertical orientation\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the accordion package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"accordion/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the accordion anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"accordion\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the accordion package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\n```\n\nThe accordion package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"accordion/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\nYou may have noticed we wrapped each accordion trigger within an `h3`. This is\nrecommended by the\n[WAI-ARIA](https://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-practices-1.1/#wai-aria-roles-states-and-properties)\ndesign pattern to ensure the accordion has the appropriate hierarchy on the\npage.\n\n### Opening multiple items\n\nSet `multiple` to `true` to allow more than one expanded item at a time.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  multiple: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Setting the initial value\n\nSet `defaultValue` to define expanded items on first render.\n\n```jsx\n// multiple mode\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  multiple: true,\n  defaultValue: [\"home\", \"about\"],\n})\n\n// single mode\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [\"home\"],\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled accordions\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` to control expanded items externally.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"accordion/controlled.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Making items collapsible\n\nSet `collapsible` to `true` to allow closing an expanded item by clicking it\nagain.\n\n\u003e Note: If `multiple` is `true`, we internally set `collapsible` to be `true`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  collapsible: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for value changes\n\nWhen the accordion value changes, the `onValueChange` callback is invoked.\n\n```jsx {2-5}\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[] }\n    console.log(\"selected accordion:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for focus changes\n\nUse `onFocusChange` to react when keyboard focus moves between item triggers.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  onFocusChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string | null }\n    console.log(\"focused item:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Horizontal orientation\n\nSet `orientation` to `horizontal` when rendering items side by side.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  orientation: \"horizontal\",\n})\n```\n\n### Disabling an accordion item\n\nTo disable a specific accordion item, pass the `disabled: true` property to the\n`getItemProps`, `getItemTriggerProps` and `getItemContentProps`.\n\nWhen an accordion item is disabled, it is skipped from keyboard navigation and\ncan't be interacted with.\n\n```jsx\n//...\n\u003cdiv {...api.getItemProps({ value: \"item\", disabled: true })}\u003e\n  \u003ch3\u003e\n    \u003cbutton {...api.getItemTriggerProps({ value: \"item\", disabled: true })}\u003e\n      Trigger\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/h3\u003e\n  \u003cdiv {...api.getItemContentProps({ value: \"item\", disabled: true })}\u003e\n    Content\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n//...\n```\n\nYou can also disable the entire accordion by setting `disabled` on the machine.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n  disabled: true,\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Open and closed state\n\nWhen an accordion item expands or collapses, `data-state` is set to `open` or\n`closed` on the item, trigger, and content elements.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the item is open or closed state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item-trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the item is open or closed state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item-content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for the item is open or closed state */\n}\n```\n\n### Focused state\n\nWhen an accordion item's trigger is focused, a `data-focus` attribute is set on\nthe item and content.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for the item's focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item-trigger\"]:focus {\n  /* styles for the trigger's focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item-content\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for the content's focus state */\n}\n```\n\n## Creating a component\n\nCreate your accordion component by abstracting the machine into your own\ncomponent.\n\n### Usage\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"accordion/component.usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Implementation\n\nUse the `splitProps` utility to separate the machine's props from the\ncomponent's props.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"accordion/component.api.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\nThe accordion's `api` exposes the following methods and properties:\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe accordion machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"accordion\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe accordion `api` exposes the following
